            WHERE [e2].[Id] = [e4].[SubmissionId]

    FROM (
        SELECT [e2].[Id], [e2].[SubmisionDate]
        FROM [Submissions] AS [e2]

    ) AS [t1]

SELECT [e].[EndTime], [e].[LessonId], [t0].[Id] AS [LessonPracticeId], [e].[Name]
FROM [Contests] AS [e]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].*
    FROM [Lessons] AS [e0]
    WHERE [e0].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t] ON [e].[LessonId] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e1].*
    FROM [Practices] AS [e1]
    WHERE [e1].[IsDeleted] = 0
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[LessonId]

FROM [Contests] AS [e]

SELECT [e].[EndTime], [e].[LessonId], [t0].[Id] AS [LessonPracticeId], [e].[Name]
FROM [Contests] AS [e]
INNER JOIN (

    FROM [Lessons] AS [e0]

SELECT [t3].[Id], [e.ExecutedTests].[Error], [e.ExecutedTests].[ExecutionResultType], [e.ExecutedTests].[Id] AS [Id0], [e.ExecutedTests].[IsCorrect], [e.ExecutedTests].[MemoryUsed], [e.ExecutedTests].[Output], [dtoExecutedTest.Test].[InputData] AS [TestInputData], [dtoExecutedTest.Test].[IsTrialTest] AS [TestIsTrialTest], [dtoExecutedTest.Test].[OutputData] AS [TestOutputData], [e.ExecutedTests].[TimeUsed], [e.ExecutedTests].[SubmissionId]
FROM [ExecutedTests] AS [e.ExecutedTests]
INNER JOIN [Tests] AS [dtoExecutedTest.Test] ON [e.ExecutedTests].[TestId] = [dtoExecutedTest.Test].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT TOP(1) [e2].[Id]
    FROM [Submissions] AS [e2]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [e3].*
        FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [e3]
        WHERE [e3].[IsDeleted] = 0
    ) AS [t1] ON [e2].[UserId] = [t1].[Id]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [e4].*
        FROM [Problems] AS [e4]
        WHERE [e4].[IsDeleted] = 0
    ) AS [t2] ON [e2].[ProblemId] = [t2].[Id]
    WHERE (([e2].[IsDeleted] = 0) AND ([e2].[IsDeleted] = 0)) AND ([e2].[Id] = @__id_0)
    ORDER BY [e2].[Id]
) AS [t3] ON [e.ExecutedTests].[SubmissionId] = [t3].[Id]
ORDER BY [t3].[Id]
